[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[35m/lib/x86_64-linux-gnu/[0m[95mlibc.so.6+0x24082[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBuildId: [0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/src/FreeRDP/winpr/include/winpr/[0m[95mstream.h[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m703:3[0m[39m in Stream_Read[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFreeRDP codebase. The issue involves an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte write operation that occurs [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter a [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m-byte allocated heap region, indicating a write operation that exceeds [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe allocated buffer boundaries. The vulnerability is triggered during the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing of an MCS [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMultipoint Communication Service[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m create request, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically in the GCC [0m[1;39m([0m[39mGeneric Conference Control[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m client network data reading [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte-write-heap-buffer-overflow. This type of vulnerability [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs when a program writes data beyond the allocated boundaries of a heap buffer,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially leading to memory corruption, crashes, or arbitrary code execution.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the following sequence:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The error occurs in `Stream_Read` function located at [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/winpr/include/winpr/[0m[95mstream.h[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m703:3[0m[39m`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This is called from `gcc_read_client_network_data` in [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/core/[0m[95mgcc.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m1875:3[0m[39m`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Which is invoked by `gcc_read_client_data_blocks` at line [0m[1;36m617[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The chain continues through `gcc_read_conference_create_request` and [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mcs_recv_connect_initial`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs when attempting to write [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes at memory address [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x519000001d60[0m[39m`, which is located exactly at the boundary [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m992[0m[39m-byte heap region that was allocated from `[0m[1;36m0x519000001980[0m[39m` to `[0m[1;36m0x519000001d60[0m[39m`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis indicates that the write operation attempts to access memory immediately [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing the allocated buffer.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe problematic buffer was allocated in:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `mcs_new` function at `[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/core/[0m[95mmcs.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m1446:34[0m[39m`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using `calloc` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich allocates and zero-initializes memory[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocation occurs during the processing of [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`freerdp_is_valid_mcs_create_request`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The vulnerability is triggered through the fuzzing test harness [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TestFuzzCoreServer`, specifically in the `test_server` function[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The issue occurs during the parsing of MCS create request data, suggesting [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimproper bounds checking when reading client network data[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The overflow happens during a `Stream_Read` operation, indicating that the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream reading logic does not properly validate that sufficient space is available [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the destination buffer[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The [0m[1;36m992[0m[39m-byte allocation size and the attempt to write [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes beyond it suggests[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma miscalculation in either the required buffer size or the amount of data being [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following components [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be investigated:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stream Reading Infrastructure** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/winpr/include/winpr/[0m[95mstream.h[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m703[0m[39m and surrounding `Stream_Read` implementation[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer bounds checking mechanisms in stream operations[0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `gcc_read_client_network_data` function at line [0m[1;36m1875[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **MCS Connection Handling** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/src/FreeRDP/libfreerdp/core/[0m[95mmcs.c[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Data Structure Definitions**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1964[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mchannel->ChannelId = channelId;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1965[0m[39m:   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1966[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1967[0m[39m:   [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchannelCount % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1968[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;35mStream_SafeSeek[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* padding *[0m[35m/[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1969[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1970[0m[39m:   [0m[39mreturn TRUE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1971[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibfreerdp/core/mcs.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m309[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m:    [0m[39mmcs->channelCount = [0m[1;35mfreerdp_settings_get_uint32[0m[1;39m([0m[39msettings, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFreeRDP_ChannelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m309[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mmcs->channelCount = CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and the ASAN report, I have identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the heap-buffer-overflow:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause: Signed/Unsigned Integer Type Mismatch[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe critical vulnerability stems from a type mismatch in the `channelCount` field:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Declaration** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs.h:[0m[1;36m147[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `INT8 channelCount;` - signed [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit integer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrange:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m-128[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m127[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Network Read** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgcc.[0m[1;92mc:1857[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mStream_Read_UINT8[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` - [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads unsigned [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-bit value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrange: [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Bounds Check** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgcc.[0m[1;92mc:1862[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompares signed INT8 value[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Loop Usage** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgcc.[0m[1;92mc:1866[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT32 i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < mcs->channelCount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcasts INT8 to UINT32[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Exploitation Scenario:**[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Attacker sends `channelCount = [0m[1;36m255[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0xFF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via fuzzing[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stored in `INT8 mcs->channelCount` as `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` due to signed interpretation[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Bounds check: `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m` evaluates to FALSE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbypassed![0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop condition: `[0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m` cast to UINT32 becomes `[0m[1;36m0xFFFFFFFF[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m294[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m967[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m295[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop attempts to access `mcs->channels[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` for massive number of iterations[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer overflow occurs when accessing beyond the allocated [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m channels [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m992[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Secondary Issue: Protocol Read/Write Mismatch[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThere's also a protocol inconsistency:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Write function** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgcc.[0m[1;92mc:1911[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mStream_Write_UINT32[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` - [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Read function** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgcc.[0m[1;92mc:1857[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mStream_Read_UINT8[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` - [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis creates incompatibility between client-side write and server-side read [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Change Field Type in Structure Definition[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `libfreerdp/core/mcs.h`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Line [0m[1;36m147[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange the `channelCount` field from signed to unsigned:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m From:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mINT8 channelCount;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUINT32 channelCount;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates signed/unsigned confusion completely[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Matches the type used in settings [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFreeRDP_ChannelCount is UINT32[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with loop iterator types [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT32[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents negative value exploits[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The additional [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes per structure instance is negligible overhead[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix Client Network Data Reading with Local Validation[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `libfreerdp/core/gcc.c`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function:** `gcc_read_client_network_data`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Lines [0m[1;36m1857[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1866[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImplement proper validation using a local variable before assignment:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current vulnerable code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1857[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1866[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStream_Read_UINT8[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockLength < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m + [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmcs->channelCount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT32 i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < mcs->channelCount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fixed code:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUINT8 channelCount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStream_Read_UINT8[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mblockLength < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m + channelCount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchannelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmcs->channelCount = channelCount;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT32 i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < channelCount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Benefits:**[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses unsigned local variable for reading from stream[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates the value before assigning to the structure field[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removes need for explicit cast in bounds check [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1859[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ensures channelCount is properly validated before any use[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains protocol compatibility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstill reads [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte from wire[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses validated local variable in loop to avoid implicit conversions[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix Protocol Consistency in Write Function[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `libfreerdp/core/gcc.c`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function:** `gcc_write_client_network_data`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Line [0m[1;36m1911[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange the write operation to match the read operation:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m From:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStream_Write_UINT32[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m To:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmcs->channelCount > UINT8_MAX[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"channelCount %"[0m[39m PRIu32 [0m[32m" exceeds UINT8_MAX"[0m[39m, mcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStream_Write_UINT8[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUINT8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mmcs->channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ensures read/write symmetry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboth use [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates that channelCount fits in UINT8 before writing[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains protocol compatibility with existing wire format[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents protocol violations[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix Server Network Data Reading[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File:** `libfreerdp/core/gcc.c`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function:** `gcc_read_server_network_data`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** Line [0m[1;36m1947[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd bounds validation before assignment:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1947[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmcs->channelCount = channelCount;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Fixed code:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchannelCount > CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"Server returned invalid channelCount: %"[0m[39m PRIu16 [0m[32m" > [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mCHANNEL_MAX_COUNT"[0m[39m, channelCount[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return FALSE;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmcs->channelCount = channelCount;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:**[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates server response before assignment[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents overflow when server sends malicious response[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with client data validation approach[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Review All Assignment Locations[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVerify that all locations assigning to `mcs->channelCount` are safe after the type [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **mcs.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m[39m** - From UINT32 settings [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe, already has bounds check at line [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m309[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **mcs.[0m[1;92mc:1444[0m[39m** - Initialization to [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **gcc.[0m[1;92mc:1947[0m[39m** - From UINT16 server response [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeds Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m fix[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **gcc.[0m[1;92mc:1857[0m[39m** - From UINT8 network stream [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcovered by Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m fix[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Why This Fix Strategy is Optimal[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserves Existing Functionality[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the same wire protocol [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte for channelCount in client data[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing valid channel configurations continue to work[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to API surface or external interfaces[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop iterations and array accesses remain unchanged[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addresses Root Cause Completely[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates the signed/unsigned type confusion[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents negative values from bypassing bounds checks[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Ensures all values are properly validated before use[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent unsigned arithmetic throughout the codebase[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Defense in Depth[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates at the point of entry [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnetwork read[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses local variables to isolate untrusted input[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Assigns to structure field only after validation[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple bounds checks prevent exploitation[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Minimal Code Impact[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Changes only the necessary type definition and critical validation points[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify fuzzing logic or harness code[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not affect test infrastructure[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Focused fixes reduce risk of introducing new bugs[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### No Side Effects[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- UINT32 is already used for loops and settings throughout the codebase[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type change is widening [0m[1;39m([0m[39mINT8 → UINT32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, safe for all positive values[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing assignments from [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m to CHANNEL_MAX_COUNT [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain valid[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No breaking changes to existing valid usage patterns[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Prevents Related Vulnerabilities[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixing the write function prevents future protocol inconsistencies[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Adding validation to server response handling prevents server-to-client exploits[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Comprehensive approach prevents similar issues in other code paths[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Notes[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The struct field type change must be applied first to avoid compilation errors[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. All validation changes should read into local variables before assignment[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The loop variables should use the validated local variable, not the struct field[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly during reading[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Existing test cases should continue to pass since valid channelCount values [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unaffected[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The fuzzer will no longer be able to trigger the vulnerability through malformed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchannelCount values[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy comprehensively addresses the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile maintaining compatibility and not modifying any fuzzing harness or test [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfrastructure.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
